 It was his promise that he would be helped in getting the job
 2015 cricket world cap main bangladesh ke khilaaf maidan main utarane ke saath hi 400waan vanade khilne vaale chauthe cricketer bane kumaar sangakaara ne iskaa jashn shatak (naabad 105 ran) ke saath manaaya or iske saath hi unka yah karnama cricket ke record book se jud gaya
 With a century, he has become the first cricketer to score a century in his 400th match
 sabase adhik vanade khilne ke maamle main ab sangakaara se aage bharat ke sachin tendulkar (463), srilanka ke sanath jayasoorya (445) or srilanka ke hi mahela jayavardhane (444) hai lekin in teenon main se kisi ne bhi apane 400wein vanade main shatak nahin lagaaya
 In this sense, Sangakkara has become the first cricketer to make this record
 CWC15: srilanka ne bangladesh ko 92 ranon se harayasangkaara kaa yah 22waan vanade shatak bhi he
 With this, he has now surpassed South Africa's Herschelle Gibbs in the number of centuries in odis with Chris Gayle of India, Virat Kohli of India and Sourav Ganguly at number four
 ab shatakon ke maamle main inase aage keval sanath jayasoorya (28), riki ponting (30) or sachin tendulkar (49) hai
 With this century, his number of runs in the World Cup has increased to 1,142
 world cap main sabase adhik ran banane vaale cricketron kii list main sangakaara ab srilanka ke arvind disilva, dakshin africa ke harshal gibs, newjiland ke stephen fleming, srilanka se saathi khilaadi jayavardhane, pakistan ke javed miyandad or australia ke adam gilcrist ko peeche chhodte hue chathe number par pahunch gaye hai
 Now Sri Lanka is only 23 runs away from becoming the highest run-scorer in the World Cup
 world cap ke dauraan abhi pichley match (afghanistan ke khilaaf) main hi wo riki ponting ko peeche chhodte hue vanade ke sabase adhik ran banane vaale duusare player bane hai or aaj ke shatak ke saath hi unke kul ranon kii sankhya 13,844 par pahunch gai he, yani sachin ke baad 14 hajaar vanade ran banane ke liye ab unhen mahaj 154 ranon kii aavashyaktaa he
 Sangakkara, who has scored more than a thousand runs in ODI cricket for the last four years with 10 centuries, has been playing ODI cricket for the last 15 years

 - isaki sahaayak nadi purna nadi he
 - It makes estuary instead of delta

 - isaki sahaayak nadiyaan he brahmani or baitarani
